= Engineering Model Go Repository Design
:toc:
:toclevels: 2
:sectnums:

== Introduction

This <<REF_IDX-DO_DO_ARCHITECTURE_MODEL,architecture models>> the engineering-model-go repository as a model-driven toolchain.
It captures authored functional intent, export surfaces, and verification-oriented traceability.
The <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> is intended to guide implementation work in this repository using stable IDs and support paths.

=== Scope and Assumptions

- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_GROUP,Functional Groups>> and <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_UNIT,Functional Units>> are the stable authored design backbone.
- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_RUNTIME_ELEMENT,Runtime elements>> and <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_CODE_ELEMENT,code elements>> are inferred from available IaC, deployment, and source artifacts.
- Inferred coverage is evidence-driven and may be partial when source metadata is missing.
- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,Requirements>> and reference indexes are provided for traceability, not as primary narrative flow.

== How To Read This Document

This document is intentionally split into two layers:

1. Concept layer: functional and view-specific architecture narratives for human understanding.
2. Evidence layer: generated requirement traceability and inferred reference indexes.

Read in this order:

1. Architecture Intent View: stable authored architecture intent and ownership boundaries.
2. Communication / Deployment / Security Views: viewpoint-specific operational behavior.
3. Traceability View: requirement mapping, evidence coverage, and confidence.
4. Reference Appendix: supporting reference IDs and inferred-source links.

++++

== Document Health Snapshot

[cols="2,1,3,1,1,1,1,4",options="header"]
|===
|View |Authored Status |Authored Status Explanation |Units in Scope |Direct Evidence Coverage |Gap Count |Heuristic Confidence |Heuristic Basis
|Architecture Intent View (`VIEW-ARCHITECTURE-INTENT`)
|in-review
|Initial repository self-model with stable top-level domains; implementation details will be expanded iteratively.
|15
|15
|0
|high
|Defaults authored units to covered; use authoredStatus as the primary publication signal.
|Security View (`VIEW-SECURITY`)
|in-review
|Security scope starts from MCP boundary and export-validation supply chain paths.
|10
|10
|7
|high
|Counts a unit as covered when explicit authored attack-vector mapping exists.
|Traceability View (`VIEW-TRACEABILITY`)
|in-review
|Traceability scope is seeded and will be tightened as requirements are added.
|8
|8
|8
|high
|Counts a unit as covered when direct inferred runtime or code evidence exists.
|State Lifecycle View (`VIEW-STATE-LIFECYCLE`)
|draft
|Captures model validity and artifact freshness lifecycle behavior.
|0
|0
|0
|n/a
|Lifecycle heuristic is currently basic; treat authoredStatus as primary signal.
|Interaction Flow View (`VIEW-INTERACTION-FLOW`)
|draft
|Core implementation workflow is captured to guide model-driven repository changes.
|3
|3
|0
|high
|Flow heuristic is step/branch-oriented; treat authoredStatus plus projection completeness as the primary signal.
|===

== Terms and Definitions

[cols="3,7",options="header"]
|===
|Term |Definition
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_ACTOR]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_ACTOR,actor>> (TERM-ACTOR)
|A person or operational role that interacts with functional units.
|[[REF_CATALOG_ACT_AI_AGENT]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ACT_AI_AGENT,ai agent>> (ACT-AI-AGENT)
|Consumes MCP outputs to plan and execute model-guided edits. Aliases:coding agent
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_ALLOCATION_TRACE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_ALLOCATION_TRACE,allocation trace>> (FU-ALLOCATION-TRACE)
|Materializes parent-to-subsystem allocation and bidirectional traceability across composed systems. Aliases:allocation
|[[REF_CATALOG_ACT_ARCHITECTURE_AUTHOR]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ACT_ARCHITECTURE_AUTHOR,architecture author>> (ACT-ARCHITECTURE-AUTHOR)
|Maintains model structure, mappings, and architecture intent. Aliases:model author
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_DECISION]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_DECISION,architecture decision>> (TERM-DECISION)
|Authored architecture decision record with status, context, decision text, and consequences.
|[[REF_CATALOG_FEAT_ARCHITECTURE_DECISION_RECORDS]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_ARCHITECTURE_DECISION_RECORDS,architecture decision records are authored>> (FEAT-ARCHITECTURE-DECISION-RECORDS)
|Feature indicating the architecture model includes first-class ADR entries. Aliases:adrs authored
|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_ARCHITECTURE_DECISION_RECORDS]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_ARCHITECTURE_DECISION_RECORDS,architecture decision records document>> (DATA-ARCHITECTURE-DECISION-RECORDS)
|Generated document containing authored architecture decision records. Aliases:adr document, decisions document
|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_ARCHITECTURE_MODEL]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_ARCHITECTURE_MODEL,architecture model>> (DATA-ARCHITECTURE-MODEL)
|Authored architecture source describing functional intent and mappings. Aliases:architecture yml
|[[REF_CATALOG_EVT_ARTIFACT_GENERATED]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_ARTIFACT_GENERATED,artifact generated event is raised>> (EVT-ARTIFACT-GENERATED)
|Event indicating one or more generated outputs were produced successfully. Aliases:artifact generated
|[[REF_CATALOG_FG_ARTIFACT_GENERATION]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_ARTIFACT_GENERATION,artifact generation>> (FG-ARTIFACT-GENERATION)
|Generation of AsciiDoc and exchange artifacts from model inputs. Aliases:generation
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_ASCIIDOC_DIAGRAM]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_ASCIIDOC_DIAGRAM,AsciiDoc diagram>> (TERM-ASCIIDOC-DIAGRAM)
|Generated diagram block, usually Mermaid, that visualizes architecture relationships in the AsciiDoc publication.

|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR,asciidoc generator>> (FU-ASCIIDOC-GENERATOR)
|Renders architecture documentation and view narratives to AsciiDoc and PDF artifacts. Aliases:engdoc
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_ASCIIDOC_SECTION]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_ASCIIDOC_SECTION,AsciiDoc section>> (TERM-ASCIIDOC-SECTION)
|Structured generated document section or row model used to render authored and inferred architecture content.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_ATTACK_VECTOR]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_ATTACK_VECTOR,attack vector>> (TERM-ATTACK-VECTOR)
|A technical misuse or attack path that targets functional, referenced, or runtime elements.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_AUTHORED_MAPPING]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_AUTHORED_MAPPING,authored mapping>> (TERM-AUTHORED-MAPPING)
|An explicit relationship declared in architecture inputs between authored or referenced elements.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_CATALOG]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_CATALOG,catalog>> (TERM-CATALOG)
|Controlled vocabulary document used to normalize model, requirement, and generated-document terminology.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_CATALOG_ENTRY]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_CATALOG_ENTRY,catalog entry>> (TERM-CATALOG-ENTRY)
|A stable catalog term with a definition and aliases for linting, linking, and generated references.
|[[REF_CATALOG_COND_CATALOG_REFERENCES_RESOLVE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_COND_CATALOG_REFERENCES_RESOLVE,catalog references resolve successfully>> (COND-CATALOG-REFERENCES-RESOLVE)
|Condition requiring all authored references to match known catalog entries. Aliases:catalog resolved
|[[REF_CATALOG_ACT_CI_PIPELINE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ACT_CI_PIPELINE,ci pipeline>> (ACT-CI-PIPELINE)
|Runs automated validation and export checks for pull requests. Aliases:ci

|An authored security, policy, or operational control used to constrain behavior and reduce risk.

|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_EVENT]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVENT,event>> (TERM-EVENT)
|An authored trigger signal that drives transitions, flow progress, or asynchronous outcomes.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> (TERM-EVIDENCE)

|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> (TERM-FLOW)

|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW_STEP]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW_STEP,flow step>> (TERM-FLOW-STEP)
|A single authored step in a flow that captures action, data in/out, references, and normal/error/async transitions.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_FUNCTIONAL_GROUP]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FUNCTIONAL_GROUP,functional group>> (TERM-FUNCTIONAL-GROUP)

|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_FUNCTIONAL_UNIT]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FUNCTIONAL_UNIT,functional unit>> (TERM-FUNCTIONAL-UNIT)

|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_STATE]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_STATE,state>> (TERM-STATE)
|An authored lifecycle state used to model transition behavior, guards, and event-driven progression.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_STRUCTURIZR_DSL]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_STRUCTURIZR_DSL,Structurizr DSL>> (TERM-STRUCTURIZR-DSL)
|Generated Structurizr DSL workspace that projects authored architecture, relationships, dynamic views, and deployment metadata.
|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_STRUCTURIZR_DSL]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_STRUCTURIZR_DSL,structurizr dsl artifact>> (DATA-STRUCTURIZR-DSL)
|Generated Structurizr workspace DSL document. Aliases:dsl
|[[REF_CATALOG_FEAT_STRUCTURIZR_EXPORT]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_STRUCTURIZR_EXPORT,structurizr export is enabled>> (FEAT-STRUCTURIZR-EXPORT)
|Feature enabling Structurizr DSL generation and validation. Aliases:dsl export
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_STRUCTURIZR_EXPORTER]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_STRUCTURIZR_EXPORTER,structurizr exporter>> (FU-STRUCTURIZR-EXPORTER)
|Exports Structurizr DSL and supports validation/static-site workflows. Aliases:engstruct
|[[REF_CATALOG_REF_STRUCTURIZR_VALIDATOR]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_STRUCTURIZR_VALIDATOR,structurizr validator>> (REF-STRUCTURIZR-VALIDATOR)
|Structurizr DSL validation runtime used to verify generated DSL. Aliases:structurizr
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_SYSTEM_COMPOSITION]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_SYSTEM_COMPOSITION,system composition>> (FU-SYSTEM-COMPOSITION)
|Resolves downward subsystem references and composes a federated system-of-systems model. Aliases:composition
|[[REF_CATALOG_FEAT_SYSTEM_COMPOSITION]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_SYSTEM_COMPOSITION,system composition is enabled>> (FEAT-SYSTEM-COMPOSITION)
|Feature enabling recursive composition of subsystem models into a system-of-systems. Aliases:system of systems
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_ASSUMPTION]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_ASSUMPTION,threat assumption>> (TERM-THREAT-ASSUMPTION)
|Authored security assumption that records scope, rationale, owner, status, and evidence.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_DRAGON_DOCUMENT]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_DRAGON_DOCUMENT,Threat Dragon document>> (TERM-THREAT-DRAGON-DOCUMENT)
|Threat Dragon JSON representation generated from the engineering model for STRIDE threat-model review.
|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_THREAT_DRAGON_JSON]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_THREAT_DRAGON_JSON,threat dragon json artifact>> (DATA-THREAT-DRAGON-JSON)
|Generated threat model artifact for OWASP Threat Dragon. Aliases:threat dragon output
|[[REF_CATALOG_REF_THREAT_DRAGON_SCHEMAS]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_THREAT_DRAGON_SCHEMAS,threat dragon schemas>> (REF-THREAT-DRAGON-SCHEMAS)
|External JSON schemas used to validate Threat Dragon exports. Aliases:threat dragon
|[[REF_CATALOG_FEAT_THREAT_EXPORT]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_THREAT_EXPORT,threat export is enabled>> (FEAT-THREAT-EXPORT)
|Feature enabling Threat Dragon and Open OTM exports. Aliases:threat modeling export
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_THREAT_EXPORTER]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_THREAT_EXPORTER,threat exporter>> (FU-THREAT-EXPORTER)
|Exports threat model views to Threat Dragon and Open OTM representations. Aliases:engdragon
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_MITIGATION]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_MITIGATION,threat mitigation>> (TERM-THREAT-MITIGATION)
|Authored mitigation record that links a threat scenario to a control, effectiveness, verification, and evidence.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_MODEL_EXPORT]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_MODEL_EXPORT,threat model export>> (TERM-THREAT-MODEL-EXPORT)
|Generated security artifact that translates authored architecture, flows, trust boundaries, threats, and mitigations into an external threat-model schema.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_OUT_OF_SCOPE]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_OUT_OF_SCOPE,threat out-of-scope decision>> (TERM-THREAT-OUT-OF-SCOPE)
|Authored decision that excludes a threat concern from current scope with reason, owner, expiry, and evidence.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_SCENARIO]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_THREAT_SCENARIO,threat scenario>> (TERM-THREAT-SCENARIO)
|Authored threat narrative that connects attack vectors, scope, flows, controls, risks, and verification evidence.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_TRACE_MARKER]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_TRACE_MARKER,trace marker>> (TERM-TRACE-MARKER)
|Source-level marker such as TRLC-LINKS or ENGMODEL-LINKS used to connect declarations to requirements and model entities.
|[[REF_CATALOG_FG_TRACEABILITY_COMPLIANCE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_TRACEABILITY_COMPLIANCE,traceability and compliance>> (FG-TRACEABILITY-COMPLIANCE)
|Requirement trace exports and compliance-oriented output generation. Aliases:compliance
|[[REF_CATALOG_FEAT_TRACEABILITY_EXPORT]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_TRACEABILITY_EXPORT,traceability export is enabled>> (FEAT-TRACEABILITY-EXPORT)
|Feature enabling TRLC and LOBSTER generation flows. Aliases:trace export
|[[REF_CATALOG_AV_TRACEABILITY_GAP_DRIFT]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_AV_TRACEABILITY_GAP_DRIFT,traceability gap drift>> (AV-TRACEABILITY-GAP-DRIFT)
|Requirement links or tests drifting from implementation over time. Aliases:trace drift
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_TRLC_EXPORTER]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_TRLC_EXPORTER,trlc exporter>> (FU-TRLC-EXPORTER)
|Exports requirements and model structures to TRLC artifacts. Aliases:engtrlc
|[[REF_CATALOG_DATA_TRLC_PACKAGE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_TRLC_PACKAGE,trlc package>> (DATA-TRLC-PACKAGE)
|Generated TRLC requirements package and model metadata. Aliases:trlc output
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_TRLC_PACKAGE]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_TRLC_PACKAGE,TRLC package>> (TERM-TRLC-PACKAGE)
|Generated TRLC model and requirements package used for formal requirement traceability processing.
|[[REF_CATALOG_REF_TRLC_TOOLCHAIN]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_REF_TRLC_TOOLCHAIN,trlc toolchain>> (REF-TRLC-TOOLCHAIN)
|TRLC parser and runtime used for requirements language validation. Aliases:trlc
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_TRUST_BOUNDARY]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_TRUST_BOUNDARY,trust boundary>> (TERM-TRUST-BOUNDARY)
|An authored trust separation zone that marks policy, identity, or security control boundaries.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_UPWARD_LINKING]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_UPWARD_LINKING,upward linking>> (TERM-UPWARD-LINKING)
|Rule where runtime and code elements point to stable functional groups/units; authored architecture does not depend on inferred IDs.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION,validation>> (TERM-VALIDATION)
|Model quality gate that checks authored documents, references, relationship semantics, and requirement lint results.
|[[REF_CATALOG_FG_VALIDATION_ANALYSIS]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_VALIDATION_ANALYSIS,validation and analysis>> (FG-VALIDATION-ANALYSIS)
|Validation, inference, and evidence analysis over authored and inferred model content. Aliases:analysis
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION_DIAGNOSTIC]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION_DIAGNOSTIC,validation diagnostic>> (TERM-VALIDATION-DIAGNOSTIC)
|Structured validation finding with code, severity, message, and optional source path.
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_VALIDATION_ENGINE]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_VALIDATION_ENGINE,validation engine>> (FU-VALIDATION-ENGINE)
|Validates IDs, references, and model consistency across authored entities and mappings. Aliases:validator
|[[REF_CATALOG_EVT_VALIDATION_FAILED]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_VALIDATION_FAILED,validation failed event is raised>> (EVT-VALIDATION-FAILED)
|Event indicating model or export validation failed. Aliases:validation failure
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_VERIFICATION_CHECK]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VERIFICATION_CHECK,verification check>> (TERM-VERIFICATION-CHECK)
|An inferred or authored verification artifact that validates requirement behavior with test evidence.
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_TERM_VIEW]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VIEW,view>> (TERM-VIEW)
|Authored projection configuration that selects roots, entity kinds, mappings, audience, and abstraction.
|[[REF_CATALOG_FU_VIEW_PROJECTION]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_VIEW_PROJECTION,view projection>> (FU-VIEW-PROJECTION)
|Builds view-specific projections for architecture communication and traceability outputs. Aliases:projection
|===

flowchart LR
  SYS["System"]:::system_boundary

  FU["Functional Unit"]:::functional_unit
  ACT(("Actor")):::actor
  REF["Referenced Element"]:::referenced_element
  IFACE[/"Interface"/]:::interface
  DATA[("Data Object")]:::data_object
  DEPT["Deployment Target"]:::deployment_target
  CTRL[["Control"]]:::control
  TB[/"Trust Boundary"\]:::trust_boundary
  ST(("State")):::state
  EVT(("Event")):::event
  FLOW{"Flow"}:::flow
  FSTEP>"Flow Step"]:::flow_step
  AV(("Attack Vector")):::attack_vector
  REQ["Requirement"]:::requirement
  VER["Verification Check"]:::verification
  RT["Runtime Element"]:::runtime_element
  DEP["Deployment Element"]:::deployment_element
  CODE["Code Element"]:::code_element

  SYS --> FG
  FG --> FU
  ACT --> FU
  FU --> REF
  FU --> IFACE
  FU --> DATA
  FU --> DEPT
  FU --> CTRL
  FU --> TB
  ST -->|triggered_by| EVT
  ST -->|guarded_by| CTRL
  FLOW --> FSTEP
  FSTEP -->|flow_ref| FU
  REQ -->|applies_to| FU
  VER -->|verifies| REQ
  VER -->|implemented_by| CODE
  FU -->|realizes| RT
  DEP --> RT
  AV --> FU
  RT -->|implemented_by| CODE
  REQ -->|code_trace| CODE

[[SEC_VIEW_VIEW-ARCHITECTURE-INTENT]]
== Architecture Intent View

Show the stable authored architecture intent: capability areas, unit ownership boundaries, and intentional responsibility split.

=== What This View Answers


- What are the main capability areas?

- What are the stable units of responsibility and what does each unit own?

- How are responsibilities intentionally split?

What this diagram shows: stable capability decomposition from functional groups into functional units.

===== CLI Orchestration (FU-CLI-ORCHESTRATION)





Command entrypoints orchestrating <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> load, <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION,validation>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_GENERATION,generation>>, and exports.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CLI_ORCHESTRATION,cli orchestration>>; includes decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR,AsciiDoc Generator>> and decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MODEL_LOADER,Model Loader>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR,AsciiDoc Generator>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MODEL_LOADER,Model Loader>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_VALIDATION_ENGINE,Validation Engine>>

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_001,REQ-EMG-001>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_003,REQ-EMG-003>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_004,REQ-EMG-004>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_005,REQ-EMG-005>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_006,REQ-EMG-006>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_009,REQ-EMG-009>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_013,REQ-EMG-013>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_014,REQ-EMG-014>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_015,REQ-EMG-015>>






===== Model Loader (FU-MODEL-LOADER)





Loads and normalizes architecture, <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_CATALOG,catalog>>, <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirements>>, and <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_DESIGN,design documents>>.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MODEL_LOADER,model loader>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

none

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_001,REQ-EMG-001>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_016,REQ-EMG-016>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_027,REQ-EMG-027>>






===== System Composition (FU-SYSTEM-COMPOSITION)





Resolves downward subsystem references from local subdirectories and composes a federated system-of-systems <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>>.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_SYSTEM_COMPOSITION,system composition>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

none

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_016,REQ-EMG-016>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_017,REQ-EMG-017>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_018,REQ-EMG-018>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_019,REQ-EMG-019>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_027,REQ-EMG-027>>

AI-agent integration and runtime API responsibilities.

	

	Exposes model-aware tools over MCP with strict input and error contracts.

===== MCP Server (FU-MCP-SERVER)





Serves model-backed tools over MCP with path safety and structured errors.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MCP_SERVER,mcp server>>; includes decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MODEL_LOADER,Model Loader>> and decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_VALIDATION_ENGINE,Validation Engine>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MODEL_LOADER,Model Loader>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_VALIDATION_ENGINE,Validation Engine>>

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_007,REQ-EMG-007>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_008,REQ-EMG-008>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_015,REQ-EMG-015>>




























<<<

[[SEC_VIEW_VIEW-SECURITY]]
== Security View

Show inferred exposure and dependency <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_RISK,risk>> points aligned to unit boundaries, focused on attack paths and security <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>>.

=== What This View Answers


- What are the main <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_TRUST_BOUNDARY,trust boundaries>> and attack paths?

- Which units are exposed and what security <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> exists?

- Where is the threat <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> incomplete?

=== Coverage Gaps

Coverage summary: 3/10 units have direct <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> coverage in this <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VIEW,view>>.


- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR,AsciiDoc Generator>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CLI_ORCHESTRATION,CLI Orchestration>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_LOBSTER_EXPORTER,LOBSTER Exporter>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_STRUCTURIZR_EXPORTER,Structurizr Exporter>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_TRLC_EXPORTER,TRLC Exporter>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_THREAT_EXPORTER,Threat Exporter>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_VALIDATION_ENGINE,Validation Engine>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.


=== Recommended Next Evidence Additions


- Add explicit authored attack-vector mappings for units currently marked without threat linkage.

- Add security signal ownership metadata (logs/alerts/<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVENT,events>>) for unresolved observability <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>>.

- Map additional security-relevant dependencies and exposures into <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_AUTHORED_MAPPING,authored mappings>> for traceable coverage.

What these diagrams show: OWASP-style context views split by functional group. Each group diagram keeps owned functional units and owned security-relevant entities inside the functional-group container; connected actors, referenced elements, external functional units, and other external entities are rendered outside it.

[[SEC_VIEW_VIEW-TRACEABILITY]]
== Traceability View

Show requirement-to-unit-to-evidence traceability, including coverage confidence and explicit <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> gaps.

=== What This View Answers


- Which <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirements>> map to which units?

- Which authored units have runtime/code <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> and which do not?

- Where are confidence or completeness gaps in trace coverage?

=== Coverage Gaps

Coverage summary: 8/8 units have direct <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> coverage in this <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VIEW,view>>.


- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR,AsciiDoc Generator>> has no direct inferred runtime <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CLI_ORCHESTRATION,CLI Orchestration>> has no direct inferred runtime <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CODEMAP_INFERENCE,Codemap Inference>> has no direct inferred runtime <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_EVIDENCE,evidence>> yet.

== Traceability Appendix

=== Requirement Details
[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_001]]
==== REQ-EMG-001

While <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_MODE_LOCAL_DEVELOPMENT,local development mode is active>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_MODEL_UPDATED,model updated event is received>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall validate <<REF_IDX-DO_DO_ARCHITECTURE_MODEL,architecture model>> before <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>.


NOTE: <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VALIDATION,Validation>> must gate all <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_GENERATION,generation>> flows.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_003]]
==== REQ-EMG-003

While <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_STATE_MODEL_VALID,model is valid>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall produce AsciiDoc architecture publication output.


NOTE: Human-readable architecture output remains required.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_004]]
==== REQ-EMG-004

Where <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_THREAT_EXPORT,threat export is enabled>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall export <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_THREAT_DRAGON_JSON,threat dragon json artifact>> plus open threat <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> artifact.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_010]]
==== REQ-EMG-010

NOTE: Identifiers are scoped per system; cross-system references are qualified by subsystem to avoid collisions.

NOTE: A subsystem is parent-agnostic; parent <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ALLOCATION,allocation>> is materialized only in composed artifacts, never written back to the child (ADR-EMG-009, ADR-EMG-011).

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_023]]
==== REQ-EMG-023

When <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall flag any <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> that links to another <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> in the same document.


NOTE: <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,Requirements>> carry no tiers. A <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> is either delegated to a subsystem through a downward <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_COMPOSITION,composition>> <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ALLOCATION,allocation>> or implemented here, and the delegation link alone tells the two apart. Linking <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirements>> to one another inside a document recreates tier coupling and is confusing across system boundaries, so it is flagged.



===== Requirement-to-Unit-to-Evidence Coverage

What this diagram shows: this requirement-to-unit mapping extended with inferred runtime/code plus verification evidence attached to each requirement and unit.

[source,mermaid]

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_026]]
==== REQ-EMG-026

Where <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_SYSTEM_COMPOSITION,system composition is enabled>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall render in the <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VIEW,view>> the delegation link from each delegated <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> to the specific subsystem <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> that satisfies it.


NOTE: A provided contract entry names (ref) the subsystem <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> that realizes it, so a parent delegation traces to exactly the <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> that satisfies it. An allocated capability with no such ref is flagged as untraceable, and a ref to a <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> the subsystem does not define is rejected.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_027]]
==== REQ-EMG-027

Where <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_SYSTEM_COMPOSITION,system composition is enabled>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall resolve an external git subsystem reference by cloning the repository into the workspace .engmod cache.


NOTE: A subsystem may reference an external repository with git (and an optional rev and path). The <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> is cloned once into .engmod/subsystems/<id> — a gitignored, temporary cache reused while it points at the same repository — and resolved like a local subsystem, giving a full cross-repository composed <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_VIEW,view>>. References stay downward-only.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_028]]
==== REQ-EMG-028

When <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall reject a code trace link that resolves to no <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> or <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> element.


NOTE: Code markers (TRLC-LINKS to a <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>>, ENGMODEL-LINKS to a <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> element) are existence-checked against the <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>>, not only shape-checked, so a link to a deleted or mistyped id is a dangling link and fails the build. A trace link is only checked for the <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> that owns its code (see <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_030,REQ-EMG-030>> scoping).

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_029]]
==== REQ-EMG-029

When <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall flag each <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> that is traced by neither code nor verification nor a downward delegation.


NOTE: An orphan <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> has no implementing code symbol, no verification, and is not delegated to a subsystem; it is a coverage gap surfaced as a warning so it is visible without breaking the build.



===== Requirement-to-Unit-to-Evidence Coverage

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_030]]
==== REQ-EMG-030

When <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall export a machine-readable traceability matrix that links each <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> to its implementing code and verification and delegated subsystem <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>>.


NOTE: One consolidated matrix (JSON) replaces having to read it out of prose and diagrams. Code is attributed to the <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> whose architecture.yml is its nearest enclosing root, so a parent <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>> never validates or counts a child <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_TERM_MODEL,model>>'s trace links (monorepo scoping).

== Gemara GRC Model

This chapter renders the model as OpenSSF Gemara (https://gemara.openssf.org) documents. Each artifact is built with the official `go-gemara` SDK types and validated against the published Gemara CUE schemas. Generate the full YAML set with `enggemara`; query it via the `gemara.*` MCP tools.

[cols="1,3,1",options="header"]
|===
|Gemara Layer |Artifact |Entries
|L1
|Vector Catalog
|4
|L1
|Principle Catalog
|5
|L1
|Guidance Catalog
|2
|L2
|Capability Catalog
|16
|L2
|Control Catalog
|3
|L2
|Threat Catalog
|2
|L3
|Risk Catalog
|3
|L3
|Policy
|2
|-
|Control→Threat Mapping
|3
|-
|Lexicon
|59
|L7
|Audit Log
|5
|L6
|Enforcement Log
|2
|===

=== Controls (L2)

[cols="2,4,2,1",options="header"]
|===
|Control |Objective |Group |Assessment Requirements
|CTRL-MCP-PATH-BOUNDARY
|Enforce repo-root path constraints and reject traversal paths in MCP tools.
|input-validation
|1
|CTRL-STRICT-MCP-INPUT-SCHEMA
|Enforce per-tool input schema and reject unknown arguments.
|input-validation
|1
|CTRL-TRACEABILITY-COVERAGE
|Require requirement-linked verification evidence for modeled behavior.
|assurance
|1
|===

=== Threats (L2)

[cols="2,4,2",options="header"]
|===
|Threat |Title |Group
|TS-MCP-PATH-TRAVERSAL
|MCP path traversal accesses non-repo files
|stride-tampering
|TS-TRACEABILITY-DRIFT
|Requirement traceability drifts from implementation
|stride-repudiation
|===

=== Risks (L3)

[cols="2,4,1",options="header"]
|===
|Risk |Title |Severity
|RISK-MCP-PATH-ESCAPE
|MCP path traversal exposes non-repository files
|High
|RISK-TRACEABILITY-DRIFT
|Traceability drift weakens assurance evidence
|Medium
|RISK-STALE-ARTIFACTS
|Stale generated artifacts misrepresent the system
|Low
|===
